Python Scripts (All Implemented)**\n\n#### **init-memorytree.py (95 lines)**\n- Creates fresh MemoryTree workspace in any repo\n- Arguments: `--root`, `--project-name`, `--goal-summary`, `--locale`, `--date`, `--time`, `--force`\n- Refuses if AGENTS.md or external policy sources exist (directs to upgrade-memorytree.py)\n- Uses `_scaffold_utils` to create directory structure and populate template files\n\n#### **upgrade-memorytree.py (306 lines)**\n- Safely adds missing MemoryTree pieces to partial repos\n- Preserves existing AGENTS.md by default\n- Outputs JSON or text format with state_before/after, created_files, preserved_files\n- Includes 9 sophisticated validation functions to check if AGENTS.md covers required concepts:\n  - alias mapping (en-usтЖТen, zh-twтЖТzh-cn, etc.)\n- `detect_repo_locale()` - inspects AGENTS.md, README.md, top-level files, docs/\n- `detect_system_locale()` - checks locale.getlocale(), LC_ALL, LANG env vars\n- CJK character detection (3400-9FFF Unicode range)\n- Latin character detection\n- Scoring system: if zh_score тЙе en_score ├Ч 1.25 тЖТ zh-cn, vice versa\n\n#### **_scaffold_utils.py (320 lines)**\n- `build_datetime()` - master function that:\n  - Copies raw file to both repo mirror and global archive\n  - Generates cleaned Markdown deterministically (no model tokens)\n  - Creates manifest JSON with metadata\n  - Upserts SQLite search index (WAL mode for concurrency)\n  - Preserves existing import_timestamp if manifest unchanged\n\n**Search Index:**\n- `upsert_search_index()` - SQLite with ON CONFLICT DO UPDATE\n- Table: transcripts (client, project, session_id, raw_sha256, ...)\n\n**Discovery:**\n- `discover_source_files()` - scans ~/.claude/projects/, ~/.codex/sessions/, ~/.gemini/tmp/\n- `transcript_matches_repo()` - matches via cwd or project slug\n- `infer_project_slug()` - extracts from cwd, Claude source path, or Gemini parent\n\n**Utilities:**\n- `slugify()` - ASCII-only, lowercase, replace non-alphanumeric with -\n- `sha256_file()` - content hash for deduplication\n- `normalize_timestamp()` - ISO 8601 with Z suffix\n- `timestamp_partition()` - YYYY/MM for directory structure\n- `yaml_escape()` - escape quotes/newlines for YAML frontmatter\n- `extract_text_blocks()` - recursively pull text from nested content\n- `extract_gemini_text()` - Gemini-specific text extraction\n- `load_jsonl()` - resilient line-by-line JSON parsing\n- `write_clean_markdown()` - generates formatted Markdown with YAML frontmatter\n\n---\n\n### **5. Configuration Files & Templates**\n\n**agents/openai.yaml** - OpenAI interface config:\n```yaml\ninterface:\n  display_name: \"MemoryTree\"\n  short_description: \"Repo memory scaffolding, deterministic transcript import...\"\n  default_prompt: \"[instructions for transcript handling, isolated PR workflow]\"\n```\n\n**Template Files (4 templates ├Ч 2 locales = 8 files):**\n\n1. **agents.md template** - Contains sections:\n   - Read Order (spec)\n   - Memory Rules (sync active todo, append-only chat logs)\n   - Transcript Rules (if enabled: archive by client/project/session, deterministic cleaning)\n   - Git Rules (MemoryTree-scoped commits, dedicated branch/PR, auto-merge conditional)\n\n2. **goal.md template** - Metadata, North Star, Scope, Acceptance Signals, Change Log\n\n3. **todo.md template** - Binding to goal version, Milestones, In Progress, Done, Pending sections\n\n4. **chat-log.md template** - Simple entry format with date/time/user/assistant\n\n---\n\n### **6. Test Coverage**\n\n**test_locale_utils.py (7 test classes, ~20 tests)**\n- Locale aliasing (en-usтЖТen, zh-hantтЖТzh-cn)\n- Repo detection (README.md scanning, CJK scoring)\n- Case insensitivity\n- Fallback behavior\n\n**test_scaffold_utils.py (11 test classes, ~45 tests)**\n- External policy detection (CODEOWNERS, commitlint, .github/CONTRIBUTING.md)\n- DateTime parsing\n- Template substitution\n- File finding (latest goal/todo/chat-log by version)\n- Scaffold creation and preservation\n\n**test_transcript_utils.py (18+ test classes)**\n- Client inference\n- Project slug matching\n- Slugification\n- Timestamp normalization\n- Transcript content validation\n\n**test_upgrade_checks.py (16 test classes, ~35 tests)**\n- AGENTS.md merge detection (tests all 9 signal functions)\n- English and Chinese variants\n- Complete and incomplete agents\n- Template validation (ensures generated templates pass merge check)\n\n---\n\n### **7. Reference Documentation**\n\n**project-detection.md:**\n- Three states: `not-installed`, `partial`, `installed`\n- Partial = AGENTS.md exists OR Memory/ exists but incomplete\n- Installed = all of > active template locale > en\n- Never rewrite existing files just to translate them\n- Keep file language stable, mirror user's discussion language in replies\n\n**update-rules.md:**\n- New goal only on scope change (not routine progress)\n- Update todo on progress/milestone/next-step change\n- Chat logs append-only\n- Move stale context to knowledge/archive\n- Move domain facts/decisions to knowledge\n\n**transcript-archive.md:**\n- Three layouts: repo mirror, global archive, and per-project storage\n- Rules: preserve raw unchanged, generate cleaned with code, keep repo mirror current-project-only\n- Global archive: ~/.memorytree/transcripts/{raw,clean,index}/\n- One-time approval per repo for raw transcript uploads\n\n**upgrade-path.md:**\n- Merge-safe: create missing Raw transcripts preserved as source of truth.\n\n2. **Non-Destructive Upgrade:** Existing AGENTS.md and policy files are preserved and validated, not overwritten.\n\n3. **Concurrent-Safe Global Archive:** Uses SQLite WAL mode for multi-project updates without corruption.\n\n4. **Repo-Scoped Mirrors:** Current project's transcripts mirrored into repo; other projects archived globally only.\n\n5. **Client Auto-Detection:** Detects Codex/Claude/Gemini from path patterns without user specification.\n\n6. **Locale Auto-Selection:** Detects from repo content (CJK character scoring) before system locale.\n\n7. **Zero Dependencies:** All scripts use only Python standard library (json, sqlite3, pathlib, re, datetime, etc.).\n\n8. **Safe Git Defaults:** Isolated PR flow, never bypasses repo rules, raw transcripts unapproved by default.\n\n---\n\n### **10. > tmux (Terminal Multiplexer) тАФ ч╗ИчлпхдНчФихЩиуАВхЬи tmux session ф╕нхРпхКичЪДш┐ЫчиЛя╝МхН│ф╜┐хЕ│щЧнч╗ИчлпчкЧхПгя╝Мш┐ЫчиЛф╗НхЬихРОхП░ш┐РшбМуАВщЪПцЧ╢хПпф╗е tmux attach хЫЮцЭецЯечЬЛуАВ

хоГщЭЮх╕╕щАВхРИх┐Гш╖│ daemonя╝МхОЯхЫая╝Ъ

| ф╝ШхК┐ | шп┤цШО |
|------|------|
| щЫ╢щЕНч╜ох╕╕щй╗ | ф╕НщЬАшжБхЖЩ systemd service цЦЗф╗╢цИЦц│ихЖМ Windows цЬНхКб |

| ш╖их╣│хП░ | Linux/macOS хОЯчФЯцФпцМБя╝МWindows щАЪш┐З WSL/Git Bash хПпчФи |
| ш╜╗щЗП | ф╕Нх╝ХхЕещвЭхдЦф╛Эш╡Ця╝МPython шДЪцЬмчЫ┤цОехЬи tmux щЗМш╖С |
| цШУф║ОчобчРЖ | хС╜хРН sessionя╝ИхжВ memorytree-daemonя╝Йя╝Мstart/stop/status ф╕АцЭбхС╜ф╗дцРЮхоЪ |

шо╛цГ│ф╕нчЪДчФиц│Хя╝Ъ

# хРпхКи
memorytree-daemon start
# хЖЕщГицЙзшбМ: tmux new-session -d -s memorytree-daemon "python heartbeat.py"

# цЯечЬЛцЧех┐Ч

# хБЬцнв
memorytree-daemon stop
# хЖЕщГицЙзшбМ: tmux send-keys -t memorytree-daemon C-c

## "щЧ╣щТЯ"цШпф╗Аф╣Ия╝Я

цпПф╕кцУНф╜Ьч│╗ч╗ЯщГ╜шЗкх╕жхоЪцЧ╢ф╗╗хКбх╖ехЕ╖я╝Мф╕НщЬАшжБхоЙшгЕф╗╗ф╜Хф╕Ьше┐я╝Ъ

| ф╜ачЪДч│╗ч╗Я | шЗкх╕жчЪД"щЧ╣щТЯ" | ф╜ачФиш┐ЗчЪДч▒╗ф╝╝ф╕Ьше┐ |
|---------|-------------|----------------|
| Linux | cron | хГПцЙЛцЬ║хоЪцЧ╢щЧ╣щТЯя╝МхЖЩф╕АшбМх░▒шбМ |
| macOS | launchd | ч│╗ч╗ЯхБПхе╜шо╛ч╜ощЗМчЪД"хРпхКищб╣" |

def auto_commit(project_path):
    os.chdir(project_path)
    
    # цгАцЯецЬЙц▓бцЬЙхПШхКи
    result = run("git status --porcelain Memory/")
    if not result.strip():
        return  # ц▓бхПШхКия╝Мш╖│ш┐З
    
    # цЬЙхПШхКия╝МцПРф║д
    run("git add Memory/")
    run('git commit -m "chore(memorytree): import transcript 2026-03-14"')
    
    # хПпщАЙя╝ЪшЗкхКи push
    if config.auto_push:
        run("git push")

     2тЖТname: memorytree-workflow
     3тЖТdescription: Detect, initialize, and maintain a reusable MemoryTree project-memory workspace for any code repository. On activation, immediately detect and report the repo's MemoryTree state.
     4тЖТ---
     5тЖТ
     6тЖТ# MemoryTree
     7тЖТ
     8тЖТUse this skill for repo-level project memory. Do not treat it as an application runtime feature unless the user explicitly asks to productize it.
     9тЖТ
    10тЖТ## On Activation
    11тЖТ
    12тЖТWhen this skill is invoked, immediately perform these steps without waiting for further user input:
    13тЖТ
    14тЖТ1. Detect the repo state (`not-installed`, `partial`, or `installed`) using `references/project-detection.md`.
    15тЖТ2. If `not-installed`: run `scripts/init-memorytree.py` to scaffold the workspace, then report what was created.
    16тЖТ3. If `partial`: run `scripts/upgrade-memorytree.py` to add missing pieces, then report what was added.
    17тЖТ4. If `installed`: read the active goal, bound todo, and latest chat log. Report the current state (goal summary, todo progress, pending tasks) and ask the user what they want to work on next.
    18тЖТ
    19тЖТDo not stop after detection to ask whether you should proceed. Act on the result immediately.
    20тЖТ
    21тЖТ## Core Behavior
    22тЖТ
    23тЖТ1. Detect the repo state before changing files. Use `references/project-detection.md`.
    24тЖТ2. If MemoryTree is missing, initialize it with `scripts/init-memorytree.py`. If the script cannot run, create the files from `assets/templates/`.
    25тЖТ3. If MemoryTree is partial, upgrade it with `scripts/upgrade-memorytree.py` before manual maintenance.
    26тЖТ4. If MemoryTree is already installed, maintain only the active goal, bound todo, and current chat log. Use `references/update-rules.md`.
    27тЖТ5. Keep the installation compatible with the host repo's branch, PR, CI, and review rules. Use `references/git-policy.md`.
    28тЖТ6. Prefer safe defaults: do not add reply suffix requirements unless the host repository already requires them, do not mix code-and-memory commits by default, and do not override branch policy. MemoryTree-only git automation is allowed only inside the isolated flow in `references/git-policy.md`.
    29тЖТ7. When locale is not explicit, choose it from repo language first, then system language. Use `references/locale-selection.md`.
    30тЖТ8. Keep reply language aligned with user language first, then repo locale. Use `references/response-language.md`.
    31тЖТ9. For partial repos, use the non-destructive upgrade path before manual maintenance. Use `references/upgrade-path.md`.
    32тЖТ10. When transcript archival is enabled, import transcripts with deterministic code, preserve raw transcripts as evidence in both the current repo mirror and the global archive, generate cleaned Markdown for indexing, keep cross-project backfills and ambiguous ownership cases in the global archive only, and ask once per repository whether raw transcript files may be committed or pushed. Use `references/transcript-archive.md`.
    33тЖТ11. When scripts are needed, prefer an existing `uv run python` environment first, then a system `python`, and only fall back to manual scaffolding or conservative manual review if no runner is available. Use `references/execution-environment.md`.
    34тЖТ
    35тЖТ## Read Order
    36тЖТ
    37тЖТ1. Repo `AGENTS.md`, if present.
    38тЖТ2. Latest file in `Memory/01_goals/`.
    39тЖТ3. Latest todo bound to that goal in `Memory/02_todos/`.
    40тЖТ4. `Memory/04_knowledge/` only when needed.
    41тЖТ5. `Memory/06_transcripts/clean/`, transcript manifests, and repo-local raw transcript mirrors only when transcript history or cross-project memory search is relevant.
    42тЖТ6. `Memory/03_chat_logs/` and `Memory/05_archive/` only when needed.
    43тЖТ
    44тЖТ## Detect
    45тЖТ
    46тЖТ1. Check whether `Memory/` exists and matches the layout in `references/memory-layout.md`.
    47тЖТ2. Classify the repo as `not-installed`, `partial`, or `installed`.
    48тЖТ3. If the repo already has stronger rules than the generated templates, preserve the repo rules and only add missing MemoryTree pieces.
    49тЖТ
    50тЖТ## Upgrade
    51тЖТ
    52тЖТ1. Use `scripts/upgrade-memorytree.py` for repositories that already have `AGENTS.md`, custom policy files, or partial `Memory/` content.
    53тЖТ2. Preserve existing repo policy files by default.
    54тЖТ3. Create only the missing MemoryTree pieces.
    55тЖТ4. Read the upgrade result and treat `agents_merge_required=true` as a manual review task, not an overwrite instruction.
    56тЖТ5. If no Python runner is available, do not create a project-local environment automatically. Fall back to conservative manual inspection and only make low-risk changes unless the user explicitly approved environment setup.
    57тЖТ
    58тЖТ## Initialize
    59тЖТ
    60тЖТ1. Run `scripts/init-memorytree.py --root <repo>` and pass `--project-name`, `--goal-summary`, and `--locale` when the user already provided them.
    61тЖТ2. Use fresh init only when the repo does not already have `AGENTS.md` or another repo policy source such as a policy-bearing `CONTRIBUTING.md`, PR templates, `CODEOWNERS`, or commitlint config. If repo policy already exists, switch to `scripts/upgrade-memorytree.py` instead of trying to skip `AGENTS.md`.
    62тЖТ3. Review the generated `AGENTS.md` before keeping it. Merge it with the repo's existing policy if needed.
    63тЖТ4. Keep the initial installation minimal: `Memory/01_goals`, `02_todos`, `03_chat_logs`, optional `04_knowledge`, `05_archive`, and `06_transcripts` only when transcript archival is enabled for the repo or needed for transcript import.
    64тЖТ5. Use the locale-specific template files in `assets/templates/<locale>/` as the source of truth for first-run scaffolding.
    65тЖТ6. Prefer `--locale auto` when the user did not request a language explicitly.
    66тЖТ7. Use `scripts/detect-memorytree-locale.py` when you need a deterministic locale check without scaffolding files.
    67тЖТ8. Prefer `uv run python` first, then a system `python`. If neither is available, create first-run files directly from `assets/templates/` instead of creating a project-local virtual environment by default.
    68тЖТ9. If transcript archival is enabled for the repo, use `scripts/import-transcripts.py` for one explicit source file and `scripts/discover-transcripts.py` when scanning local client stores. Matching transcripts must update both the repo mirror and the global archive, while unrelated projects, ambiguous ownership cases, or mismatched explicit sources are archived in the global archive only. Let the scripts generate cleaned transcripts deterministically without spending model tokens on the cleaning step.
    69тЖТ10. Ask once whether raw transcript files may also be committed to the repository. Record the answer in `AGENTS.md`, keep the files in the repo either way, and exclude `raw` files from automatic staging until the user says yes.
    70тЖТ
    71тЖТ## Maintain
    72тЖТ
    73тЖТ1. Change the active goal only after explicit user confirmation of a scope or requirement change.
    74тЖТ2. Update the active todo when progress changes, milestones move, or the next task becomes clearer.
    75тЖТ3. Append chat logs only. Never rewrite or delete prior entries.
    76тЖТ4. Keep active files small. Move stale context to archive or knowledge files instead of bloating the active goal or todo.
    77тЖТ5. Treat product ideas, architecture decisions, and operating constraints as goal or knowledge content. Treat step-by-step execution state as todo content.
    78тЖТ6. Treat cleaned transcript indexes as discovery aids, not as the final source of truth. When exact wording matters, confirm against the raw transcript archive.
    79тЖТ7. Prefer deterministic script-based transcript cleaning over manual rewriting. Do not spend model tokens to restate or normalize transcript content when `scripts/import-transcripts.py` can do it.
    80тЖТ8. Reply in the user's language when clear; otherwise align with repo locale without rewriting existing files just to translate them.
    81тЖТ
    82тЖТ## Git And Safety
    83тЖТ
    84тЖТ1. Never assume MemoryTree can override the repo's branch model.
    85тЖТ2. Default to isolated MemoryTree-only Git operations: stage only MemoryTree-owned files, use a MemoryTree-scoped commit title, push to a dedicated branch, and open a dedicated PR.
    86тЖТ3. Enable auto-merge only for MemoryTree-only PRs, and only when the repository still enforces its required review and CI checks.
    87тЖТ4. Keep repo-local raw transcript mirrors and the global transcript archive synchronized on every import. The global index must remain safe for concurrent multi-project updates.
    88тЖТ5. Keep the repository mirror limited to transcripts that belong to the current repository. Unrelated or ambiguous transcripts belong in the global archive only.
    89тЖТ6. Keep raw transcript files under `Memory/06_transcripts/raw/**` in the repo, but exclude them from automatic staging until the user explicitly approved raw transcript uploads for that repository.
    90тЖТ7. If the diff mixes product code, shared policy files, cross-project transcript archives, or unclear ownership, stop and ask the user before committing or pushing.
    91тЖТ8. If the repo has protected branches or PR-only rules, follow them even if older MemoryTree rules say otherwise.
    92тЖТ

   102тЖТ- `references/upgrade-path.md`: safe adoption flow for partial repos.
   103тЖТ- `references/execution-environment.md`: how to run MemoryTree scripts without assuming a project-local Python environment.

   107тЖТ- `scripts/import-transcripts.py`: import one transcript into the repo mirror and global archive, then generate clean Markdown deterministically by code.
   108тЖТ- `scripts/upgrade-memorytree.py`: safely add missing MemoryTree pieces to a partial repository.
   109тЖТ- `scripts/init-memorytree.py`: deterministic scaffold script.

     2тЖТ
     3тЖТUse this file when the user wants MemoryTree to preserve local AI chat history from Codex, Claude Code, or Gemini CLI.
     4тЖТ
     5тЖТ## Goal
     6тЖТ
     7тЖТKeep a trustworthy transcript record by preserving the current project's transcript mirror and a synchronized global archive at the same time, without mixing unrelated projects into the current repository.
     8тЖТ
     9тЖТ## Core Rules
    10тЖТ
    11тЖТ1. Preserve raw transcripts unchanged as the source of truth.
    12тЖТ2. Generate cleaned Markdown transcript indexes for discovery, lightweight review, and cross-project search.
    13тЖТ3. Keep both the current repository mirror and the user-level global archive updated on every transcript import.
    14тЖТ4. Keep the repository mirror scoped to the current project only. When batch discovery sees other projects, archive them in the global archive only.
    15тЖТ5. If current-project ownership is ambiguous, treat the transcript as global-only until stronger evidence exists.
    16тЖТ6. Ask once per repository whether raw transcript files may also be committed and pushed with MemoryTree.
    17тЖТ7. Record that repository-specific answer in `AGENTS.md`.
    18тЖТ8. If the answer is not an explicit yes, keep raw transcripts in the repository mirror but exclude them from automatic staging and push.
    19тЖТ9. Use deterministic code for transcript cleaning. Do not spend model tokens to normalize transcript content when a parser script can do it.
    20тЖТ
    21тЖТ## Import Script
    22тЖТ
    23тЖТUse `scripts/import-transcripts.py` for one known source file.
    24тЖТ
    25тЖТThe script must:
    26тЖТ
    27тЖТ1. Copy the raw transcript into the current repository mirror only when the source belongs to the current repository.
    28тЖТ2. Copy the raw transcript into the global archive.
    29тЖТ3. Generate the cleaned Markdown transcript in both places with deterministic code when the source matches the current repository, or in the global archive only when it does not.
    30тЖТ4. Write manifests and update the global search index in the same operation.
    31тЖТ5. Use a concurrency-safe global index, such as SQLite WAL mode, so multiple projects can update the global archive without corrupting it.
    32тЖТ6. Refuse snapshot-only or otherwise content-empty sources instead of archiving empty transcript shells.
    33тЖТ7. Treat missing or fuzzy project signals as not matched; do not mirror them into the repository on name similarity alone.
    34тЖТ
    35тЖТ## Discovery Script
    36тЖТ
    37тЖТUse `scripts/discover-transcripts.py` when MemoryTree should scan the supported local client stores automatically.
    38тЖТ
    39тЖТThe script must:
    40тЖТ
    41тЖТ1. Discover supported transcript files from local Codex, Claude Code, and Gemini stores.
    42тЖТ2. Mirror transcripts that belong to the current repository into both the repository and the global archive.
    43тЖТ3. Backfill transcripts from unrelated projects into the global archive only.
    44тЖТ4. Skip unreadable or malformed transcript files without aborting the full discovery run.
    45тЖТ5. Skip snapshot-only or otherwise content-empty files instead of generating empty clean transcripts.
    46тЖТ6. Keep deterministic cleaning, manifest generation, and global index updates in the same operation.
    47тЖТ7. Support a current-project-only mode when the user wants to avoid global backfill during that run.
    48тЖТ8. Keep ambiguous ownership cases out of the repository mirror unless path-level evidence confirms they belong to the current repo.
    49тЖТ
    50тЖТ## Global Archive Layout
    51тЖТ
    52тЖТRecommended user-level layout:
    53тЖТ
    54тЖТ```text
    55тЖТ~/.memorytree/transcripts/
    56тЖТ  raw/
    57тЖТ    codex/<project>/<yyyy>/<mm>/<session-id>.jsonl
    58тЖТ    claude/<project>/<yyyy>/<mm>/<session-id>.jsonl
    59тЖТ    gemini/<project>/<yyyy>/<mm>/<session-id>.json
    60тЖТ  clean/
    61тЖТ    codex/<project>/<yyyy>/<mm>/<session-id>.md
    62тЖТ    claude/<project>/<yyyy>/<mm>/<session-id>.md
    63тЖТ    gemini/<project>/<yyyy>/<mm>/<session-id>.md
    64тЖТ  index/
    65тЖТ    sessions.jsonl
    66тЖТ    search.sqlite
    67тЖТ```
    68тЖТ
    69тЖТPath roots:
    70тЖТ
    71тЖТ- Windows: `%USERPROFILE%`
    72тЖТ- macOS and Ubuntu: `$HOME`
    73тЖТ
    74тЖТ## Project Mirror Layout
    75тЖТ
    76тЖТInside a repository, keep the current project's full mirror:
    77тЖТ
    78тЖТ```text
    79тЖТMemory/06_transcripts/
    80тЖТ  clean/<client>/
    81тЖТ  manifests/
    82тЖТ  raw/<client>/
    83тЖТ```
    84тЖТ
    85тЖТDo not place other projects' transcript mirrors inside the current repository.
    86тЖТ
    87тЖТ## Client Sources
    88тЖТ
    89тЖТ### Codex
    90тЖТ
    91тЖТ- Prefer full session files from `~/.codex/sessions/**/rollout-*.jsonl`.
    92тЖТ- Use `~/.codex/session_index.jsonl` for session discovery when helpful.
    93тЖТ- Treat `~/.codex/history.jsonl` as lightweight history, not the preferred full transcript source.
    94тЖТ
    95тЖТ### Claude Code
    96тЖТ
    97тЖТ- Prefer `transcript_path` when the client exposes it.
    98тЖТ- Otherwise prefer `~/.claude/projects/<project>/*.jsonl`.
    99тЖТ- Treat `~/.claude/history.jsonl` as lightweight history, not the preferred full transcript source.
   100тЖТ- Remember that local transcript retention may be limited by the client's cleanup policy.
   101тЖТ
   102тЖТ### Gemini CLI
   103тЖТ
   104тЖТ- Gemini transcript import is supported, but availability depends on saved chats or enabled checkpointing.
   105тЖТ- Prefer saved chat or resume-friendly sources first.
   106тЖТ- If checkpointing is enabled, use the checkpoint history under `~/.gemini/tmp/<project_hash>/checkpoints` and related Git snapshots under `~/.gemini/history/<project_hash>`.
   107тЖТ- If no saved chat or checkpoint source exists, report that no importable Gemini transcript is currently available.
   108тЖТ
   109тЖТ## Import Rules
   110тЖТ
   111тЖТ1. Store the raw source unchanged in the global archive, and in the current repository only when the transcript belongs to that repository.
   112тЖТ2. Compute and record a content hash for the raw file.
   113тЖТ3. Generate a cleaned Markdown file with deterministic code, not model-generated paraphrasing.
   114тЖТ4. During batch discovery, mirror only current-project transcripts into the repository. Unrelated projects go to the global archive only.
   115тЖТ5. Each cleaned Markdown file must include:
   116тЖТ   - client
   117тЖТ   - project
   118тЖТ   - session id
   119тЖТ   - start time
   120тЖТ   - cwd or repo path when available
   121тЖТ   - branch when available
   122тЖТ   - raw source path
   123тЖТ   - raw content hash
   124тЖТ6. Keep user messages, assistant messages, and useful tool summaries in the cleaned transcript.
   125тЖТ7. Drop or fold noisy events such as queue operations, repeated metadata, telemetry, and large low-signal tool dumps.
   126тЖТ8. Never treat the cleaned transcript as stronger evidence than the raw transcript.
   127тЖТ
   128тЖТ## Search Rules
   129тЖТ
   130тЖТWhen the user asks to search all memories or all chat history:
   131тЖТ
   132тЖТ1. Search the global cleaned transcript index first.
   133тЖТ2. Use the matching raw transcript files for exact confirmation.
   134тЖТ3. Then combine those results with the active repository's `Memory/` files when answering.
   135тЖТ
   136тЖТ## Git Rules
   137тЖТ
   138тЖТ1. Cleaned transcript indexes may be committed as MemoryTree-owned documentation for the current repository.
   139тЖТ2. Raw transcript files stay in the current repository mirror regardless of upload approval.
   140тЖТ3. Raw transcript files may be staged, committed, and pushed only after the user explicitly approved raw transcript uploads for that repository.
   141тЖТ4. Even when raw transcript uploads are approved, keep the PR limited to the current repository's transcript mirror. Do not mix transcript files from unrelated projects.
   142тЖТ

1тЖТ# Git Policy
     2тЖТ
     3тЖТMemoryTree must adapt to the host repository. It does not get to override it.
     4тЖТ
     5тЖТ## Safe Defaults
     6тЖТ
     7тЖТ- Do not mix MemoryTree-owned changes with product code changes by default.
     8тЖТ- Do not stage or push unrelated user work.
     9тЖТ- Do not assume direct commits to protected branches are allowed.
    10тЖТ- Do not bypass review, CI, E2E, or release controls.
    11тЖТ- Keep raw transcript files in the current project's transcript mirror by default, but exclude them from automatic staging unless the user explicitly approved raw transcript uploads for the current repository.
    12тЖТ- Do not mirror or stage transcript files from unrelated projects inside the current repository.
    13тЖТ
    14тЖТ## Policy Merge
    15тЖТ
    16тЖТWhen the repo already has branch or PR rules:
    17тЖТ
    18тЖТ1. Keep the repo's stricter rule.
    19тЖТ2. Treat MemoryTree as documentation and process support.
    20тЖТ3. Only add MemoryTree-specific guidance that does not weaken repo controls.
    21тЖТ
    22тЖТ## MemoryTree-Owned Files
    23тЖТ
    24тЖТDefault whitelist:
    25тЖТ
    26тЖТ- `Memory/**`, except `Memory/06_transcripts/raw/**` until the user explicitly approved raw transcript uploads for this repository
    27тЖТ- `AGENTS.md` only when the file is managed by MemoryTree or the user approved the merge
    28тЖТ
    29тЖТIf the diff includes files outside this whitelist, stop and ask before staging or pushing.
    30тЖТ
    31тЖТ## Default MemoryTree Flow
    32тЖТ
    33тЖТUse this flow only for MemoryTree-only changes and only when the host repo does not forbid it:
    34тЖТ
    35тЖТ1. Stage only the MemoryTree-owned files created or updated by the skill.
    36тЖТ2. Create or reuse a dedicated branch such as `memorytree/<scope>-<yyyymmdd>-<slug>`.
    37тЖТ3. Use a MemoryTree-scoped commit title. Prefer `memorytree(<scope>): <subject>`, but if the host repo enforces a commit convention, use a compatible equivalent such as `docs(memorytree): <subject>`.
    38тЖТ4. Push that dedicated branch if the repository allows the current actor to push.
    39тЖТ5. Open a dedicated PR instead of merging directly into a protected branch.
    40тЖТ6. Enable auto-merge only when the repository still enforces its required approvals and checks.
    41тЖТ7. If transcript files are included, keep the PR scoped to one repository's transcript mirror only. Do not mix cross-project transcript archives into the same PR.
    42тЖТ8. Keep the global transcript archive updated in the same import operation, but never stage or push that user-level global archive as part of a repo PR.
    43тЖТ
    44тЖТ## Commit Guidance
    45тЖТ
    46тЖТ- Keep the title concise and specific.
    47тЖТ- Prefer scopes such as `agents`, `goals`, `todos`, `chat-logs`, `transcripts`, `knowledge`, `archive`, `policy`, or `bootstrap`.
    48тЖТ- If a body is needed, keep it lightweight: reason, affected files, and whether the change is MemoryTree-only.
    49тЖТ- If the host repo requires Conventional Commits or another enforced prefix, keep `memorytree` visible as the scope or memory tag rather than bypassing the repo rule.
    50тЖТ
    51тЖТExample title:
    52тЖТ
    53тЖТ```text
    54тЖТmemorytree(todos): sync active todo progress
    55тЖТ```
    56тЖТ
    57тЖТHost-compatible example:
    58тЖТ
    59тЖТ```text
    60тЖТdocs(memorytree): sync active todo progress
    61тЖТ```
    62тЖТ
    63тЖТExample body:
    64тЖТ
    65тЖТ```text
    66тЖТReason:
    67тЖТ- align the active todo with confirmed progress
    68тЖТ
    69тЖТFiles:
    70тЖТ- Memory/02_todos/todo_v001_003_20260314.md
    71тЖТ- Memory/03_chat_logs/2026-03-14_09-30.md
    72тЖТ
    73тЖТNotes:
    74тЖТ- memorytree-only change
    75тЖТ- no product code included
    76тЖТ```
    77тЖТ
    78тЖТ## PR Guidance
    79тЖТ
    80тЖТ- Reuse the commit title as the PR title when it still describes the change accurately.
    81тЖТ- Keep the PR scoped to MemoryTree-owned files only.
    82тЖТ- State whether the PR is MemoryTree-only and whether auto-merge was enabled.
    83тЖТ- State whether raw transcripts were included or intentionally left unstaged in the repo mirror.
    84тЖТ- Follow the repository's required target branch, review policy, and CI gates.
    85тЖТ
    86тЖТ## Stop And Ask
    87тЖТ
    88тЖТStop and ask the user before committing, pushing, or opening a PR when any of these are true:
    89тЖТ
    90тЖТ1. The diff touches product code or files outside the MemoryTree whitelist.
    91тЖТ2. `AGENTS.md` has user-managed policy content that cannot be safely merged automatically.
    92тЖТ3. The target branch, base branch, or PR destination is unclear.
    93тЖТ4. The repository forbids bot pushes, automated PRs, or auto-merge.
    94тЖТ5. The repository's review or CI rules conflict with the default MemoryTree-only flow.
    95тЖТ6. Raw transcript upload permission for the repository is unknown.
    96тЖТ7. The diff includes raw transcripts or cleaned transcript indexes from other projects.

1тЖТ# Execution Environment
     2тЖТ
     3тЖТUse this file when MemoryTree needs to run a bundled Python script inside an arbitrary repository.
     4тЖТ
     5тЖТ## Goal
     6тЖТ
     7тЖТRun MemoryTree tooling without assuming the target repository already has a Python environment and without polluting the repository by default.
     8тЖТ
     9тЖТ## Preferred Order
    10тЖТ
    11тЖТ1. Use `uv run python ...` when `uv` is already available on the host machine.
    12тЖТ2. Otherwise use a working system `python`.
    13тЖТ3. If neither runner is available:
    14тЖТ   - for fresh init, fall back to direct template scaffolding from `assets/templates/`
    15тЖТ   - for upgrade or detection, fall back to conservative manual review and only make low-risk changes
    16тЖТ4. Ask the user before creating a project-local virtual environment, installing Python, or adding Python tooling files to the repository.
    17тЖТ
    18тЖТ## Why
    19тЖТ
    20тЖТ- MemoryTree is a repo-level memory workflow, not a language-specific build tool.
    21тЖТ- Many target repositories are not Python projects.
    22тЖТ- Auto-creating `.venv`, `pyproject.toml`, lockfiles, or other tooling files can pollute the host repository and conflict with its workflow.
    23тЖТ
    24тЖТ## Fresh Init
    25тЖТ
    26тЖТFor `scripts/init-memorytree.py` and first-run scaffolding:
    27тЖТ
    28тЖТ- Prefer running the script through `uv run python` or system `python`.
    29тЖТ- If no runner exists, create the initial files directly from `assets/templates/<locale>/`.
    30тЖТ- Do not block first-run installation only because Python is unavailable.
    31тЖТ
    32тЖТ## Upgrade And Detection
    33тЖТ
    34тЖТFor `scripts/upgrade-memorytree.py` and `scripts/detect-memorytree-locale.py`:
    35тЖТ
    36тЖТ- Prefer running the script through `uv run python` or system `python`.
    37тЖТ- If no runner exists, do not silently create a new environment inside the project.
    38тЖТ- Fall back to manual detection using the reference docs and keep the change set minimal.
    39тЖТ- If correct upgrade behavior depends on repo-specific policy interpretation, ask the user before proceeding.
    40тЖТ
    41тЖТ## Stop And Ask
    42тЖТ
    43тЖТStop and ask the user before environment setup when any of these are true:
    44тЖТ
    45тЖТ1. `uv` is unavailable and `python` is unavailable.
    46тЖТ2. Running the scripts would require creating a new `.venv` or installing host tooling.
    47тЖТ3. The repo has policies about local tooling, bootstrap scripts, or checked-in environment files.
    48тЖТ4. The upgrade is risky enough that manual fallback would be error-prone.
    49тЖТ

Silently registering a scheduled task without user confirmation\n2. Pushing to a repository that has no remote configured\n3. Overwriting an existing scheduled task registration from another MemoryTree version\n```\n\n#### File 2: `references/global-configuration.md` (NEW, target ~70-80 lines)\n\n**Purpose**: Document the full `~/.memorytree/` directory layout and `config.toml` schema. Single source of truth for all global-level paths.\n\n**Structure**:\n\n```\n# Global Configuration\n\nUse this file when reading or modifying MemoryTree's user-level global configuration.\n\n## Goal\n- One sentence: Provide a single user-level location for MemoryTree's global state, configuration, and cross-project data.\n\n## Directory Layout\n\n~/.memorytree/\n  config.toml          # Global configuration (heartbeat interval, watch dirs, projects, auto_push)\n  alerts.json          # Accumulated error notifications for Skill activation display\n  heartbeat.lock       # Lock file for single-instance enforcement\n  logs/\n    heartbeat.log      # Daily-rotated heartbeat execution log\n  transcripts/         # Global transcript archive (already documented in transcript-archive.md)\n    raw/\n    clean/\n    index/\n\nNote: Path roots: Windows %USERPROFILE%, macOS/Linux $HOME.\n\n## config.toml Schema\n- heartbeat_interval: integer, seconds between runs (default: 300)\n- watch_dirs: list of strings, client transcript directories to scan\n  - default: [\"~/.claude/projects/\", \"~/.codex/sessions/\", \"~/.gemini/\"]\n- projects: list of objects, registered project roots\n  - each entry: { root = \"/path/to/repo\" }\n  - auto-discovered on first Skill activation per repo, or manual add\n- auto_push: boolean (default: true) тАФ push Memory commits to remote automatically\n  - Rationale: memory is a user asset; local-only storage is an unrecoverable loss risk\n  - First install prompts user to confirm; after confirmation, silent execution\n- log_level: string, one of \"debug\", \"info\", \"warning\", \"error\" (default: \"info\")\n\n## alerts.json\n- Array of alert objects: { timestamp, project, type, message, count }\n- Written by heartbeat when errors accumulate (e.g., push fails N consecutive times)\n- Read and displayed by Skill on activation, then cleared after display\n- Types: push_failed, no_remote, lock_timeout, sensitive_info_detected\n\n## Project Registration\n- Automatic: Skill activation in a new repo adds it to projects list\n- Manual: user edits config.toml directly\n- Unregistered repos are skipped by heartbeat\n\n## Stop And Ask\nStop and ask before any of these:\n1. Modifying config.toml on behalf of the user without confirmation\n2. Clearing alerts.json without displaying alerts to the user first\n3. Adding a project to the registered list when the repo has no Memory/ directory\n```\n\n---\n\n### Phase 2: Update Existing Files (depends on Phase 1 for reference targets)\n\nThese changes can be done in any order within Phase 2, since they all reference the two new files from Phase 1. However, I recommend the order below because SKILL.md is the master specification and git-policy.md is the second most authoritative.\n\n#### File 3: `SKILL.md` тАФ Update (currently 109 lines, target <=140 lines)\n\nThe budget is tight (add ~30 lines). The heartbeat process pushes MemoryTree-owned commits to the current branch's remote automatically after each commit.\n2. Push targets the current branch. The heartbeat does not create branches or PRs; it commits directly to the branch the project is on.\n3. Before push, verify the remote exists. If no remote is configured, skip push and write an alert to `~/.memorytree/alerts.json`.\n4. On push failure (network error, auth failure, rejected push), log the error, increment failure counter, and retry on the next heartbeat run. After N consecutive failures, write an alert.\n5. First install prompts the user to confirm auto_push behavior. After confirmation, execution is silent.\n\nWhen `auto_push` is `false`:\n\n1. The heartbeat still commits locally but does not push.\n2. The user is responsible for pushing MemoryTree changes manually.\n\nRationale: Memory is a user asset. Local-only storage means a single disk failure loses all memory permanently. Auto push is the safe default.\n```\n\n**Modify \"Stop And Ask\" section**: Add item 8:\n- 8. `auto_push` is `true` but the push target branch is a protected branch that rejects direct pushes.\n\n**Total addition**: ~18 lines, bringing it to ~115 lines.\n\n#### File 5: `references/transcript-archive.md` тАФ Update (currently 142 lines, target ~150 lines)\n\n**Search Rules section (lines 130-134)** -- Clarify the search API:\n\nReplace the current 3-point Search Rules with a more specific version:\n\n```\n## Search Rules\n\nWhen the user asks to search all memories or all chat history:\n\n1. Query the global SQLite search index at `~/.memorytree/transcripts/index/search.sqlite` first.\n2. Use the JSONL session index at `~/.memorytree/transcripts/index/sessions.jsonl` for session-level metadata lookups.\n3. For matches, load the cleaned Markdown file for context. Use the raw transcript for exact-wording confirmation.\n4. Combine transcript search results with the active repository's `Memory/` files (goals, todos, knowledge) when answering.\n5. If the search index does not exist or is empty, fall back to scanning `~/.memorytree/transcripts/clean/` directory tree directly.\n```\n\n**Add a note in \"Global Archive Layout\" section (after line 67)**: Add one line referencing the new config doc:\n- \"For the full `~/.memorytree/` directory layout including config, alerts, and logs, see `references/global-configuration.md`.\"\n\n**Total change**: ~5 net new lines (replace 3 rules with 5, add 1 cross-reference), bringing it to ~146 lines.\n\n#### File 6: `assets/templates/en/agents.md` тАФ Update (currently 32 lines, target ~42 lines)\n\n**Add a new section \"Heartbeat Rules\" after \"Git Rules\"**:\n\n```\n## Heartbeat Rules\n- Transcript discovery, import, cleaning, and git push are handled by the background heartbeat, not the model.\n- The model writes only chat-log summaries and goal/todo state updates during a session.\n- If `~/.memorytree/alerts.json` contains pending alerts, display them to the user at session start.\n- If `memorytree-daemon` is not registered as a scheduled task, suggest the user run `memorytree-daemon install`.\n```\n\n**Modify \"Git Rules\" section**: Add one bullet:\n- \"When `auto_push` is enabled in `~/.memorytree/config.toml`, the heartbeat pushes MemoryTree commits automatically.
